initViewMode() {\n  jQuery('[data-view-holder]').each(function() {\n    var list = jQuery(this);\n    var holder = jQuery(list.data('view-holder'));\n    var links = list.find('[data-class-holder]');\n    var activeClass = 'active';\n    var counter = 0;\n    var prevClass, index;\n\n\n    if(!holder.length) return;\n\n    function addFirtstLinkClass() {\n      links.eq(0).addClass(activeClass);\n      holder.addClass(links.eq(0).data('classHolder'));\n      changeRowTruncate(links.eq(0));\n    }\n\n    function changeRowTruncate(target) {\n      var dataEllipsis = target.data('rowEllipsis');\n      \n      initTruncate(holder, dataEllipsis);\n      \n    }\n\n    if(links.hasClass(activeClass)){\n      links.each(function(i) {\n      var link = jQuery(this);\n\n      if(link.hasClass(activeClass)){\n        index = i;\n        counter++;\n      }\n    });\n\n    if(counter === 1){\n      var data = links.eq(index).data('classHolder');\n\n      holder.addClass(data);\n      prevClass = data;\n       changeRowTruncate(links.eq(index));\n      } else {\n        links.removeClass(activeClass);\n        addFirtstLinkClass();\n      }\n    } currentLink.addClass(activeClass);\n        holder.addClass(data);\n        prevClass = data;\n        changeRowTruncate(currentLink);\n      }\n    });\n  });\n}\n\n\n/*\n * Simple Mobile Navigation\n */\n;(function($) {\n  function MobileNav(options) {\n    this.options = $.extend({\n      container: null,\n      hideOnClickOutside: false,\n      menuActiveClass: 'nav-active',\n      menuOpener: '.nav-opener',\n      menuDrop: '.nav-drop',\n      toggleEvent: 'click',\n      outsideClickEvent: 'click touchstart pointerdown MSPointerDown'\n    }, options);\n isOpened: function() {\n      return this.container.hasClass(this.options.menuActiveClass);\n    },\n    show: function() {\n      this.container.addClass(this.options.menuActiveClass);\n      if(this.options.hideOnClickOutside) {\n        this.page.on(this.options.outsideClickEvent, this.outsideClickHandler);\n      }\n    },\n    hide: function() {\n      this.container.removeClass(this.options.menuActiveClass);\n      if(this.options.hideOnClickOutside) {\n        this.page.off(this.options.outsideClickEvent, this.outsideClickHandler);\n      }\n    },\n    toggle: function() {\n      if(this.isOpened()) {\n        this.hide();\n      } else {\n        this.show();\n      }\n    },\n    destroy: function() {\n      this.container.removeClass(this.options.menuActiveClass);\n      this.opener.off(this.options.toggleEvent, this.clickHandler);\n      this.page.off(this.options.outsideClickEvent, this.outsideClickHandler);\n    }\n  };\n\n  var activateResizeHandler = function() {\n    var win = $(window),\n      doc = $('html'),\n      resizeClass = 'resize-active',\n      flag, timer;\n doc.addClass(resizeClass);\n      }\n      clearTimeout(timer);\n      timer = setTimeout(removeClassHandler, 500);\n    };\n    win.on('resize orientationchange', resizeHandler);\n  };\n\n '.popup',\n      btnOpen: '.open',\n      btnClose: '.close',\n      openClass: 'popup-active',\n      clickEvent: 'click',\n      mode: 'click',\n      hideOnClickLink: true,\n      hideOnClickOutside: true,\n      delay: 50\n    }, opt);\n    if(this.options.holder) {\n      this.holder = $(this.options.holder);\n      this.init();\n    }\n  }\n  ContentPopup.prototype = {\n    init: function() {\n      this.findElements();\n      this.attachEvents();\n    },\n    findElements: function() {\n      this.popup = this.holder.find(this.options.popup);\n      this.btnOpen = this.holder.find(this.options.btnOpen);\n      this.btnClose = this.holder.find(this.options.btnClose);\n    },\n    attachEvents: function() {\n      // handle popup openers\n      var self = this;\n      this.clickMode = isTouchDevice || (self.options.mode === self.options.clickEvent);\n\n      if(this.clickMode) {\n        // handle click mode\n        this.btnOpen.bind(self.options.clickEvent, function(e) {\n          if(self.holder.hasClass(self.options.openClass)) {\n            if(self.options.hideOnClickLink) {\n              self.hidePopup();\n            }\n          } else {\n            self.showPopup();\n          }\n          e.preventDefault();\n        });\n\n        // prepare outside click handler\n        this.outsideClickHandler = this.bind(this.outsideClickHandler, this);\n      } else {\n        // handle hover mode\n        var timer, delayedFunc = function(func) {\n          clearTimeout(timer);\n          timer = setTimeout(function() {\n            func.call(self);\n          }, self.options.delay);\n        };\n        this.btnOpen.bind('mouseover', function() {\n          delayedFunc(self.showPopup);\n        }).bind('mouseout', function() {\n          delayedFunc(self.hidePopup);\n        });\n        this.popup.bind('mouseover', function() {\n          delayedFunc(self.showPopup);\n        }).bind('mouseout', function() {\n          delayedFunc(self.hidePopup);\n        });\n      }\n\n      // handle close buttons\n      this.btnClose.bind(self.options.clickEvent, function(e) {\n        self.hidePopup();\n        e.preventDefault();\n      });\n    },\n    outsideClickHandler: function(e) {\n      // hide popup if clicked outside\n      var targetNode = $((e.changedTouches ? e.changedTouches[0] : e).target);\n      if(!targetNode.closest(this.popup).length && !targetNode.closest(this.btnOpen).length) {\n        this.hidePopup();\n      }\n    },\n    showPopup: function() {\n      // reveal popup\n      this.holder.addClass(this.options.openClass);\n      this.popup.css({display:'block'});\n\n      // outside click handler\n      if(this.clickMode && this.options.hideOnClickOutside && !this.outsideHandlerActive) {\n        this.outsideHandlerActive = true;\n        $(document).bind('click touchstart', this.outsideClickHandler);\n      }\n    },\n    hidePopup: function() {\n      // hide popup\n      this.holder.removeClass(this.options.openClass);\n      this.popup.css({display:'none'});\n\n      // outside click handler\n      if(this.clickMode && this.options.hideOnClickOutside && this.outsideHandlerActive) {\n        this.outsideHandlerActive = false;\n        $(document).unbind('click touchstart', this.outsideClickHandler);\n      }\n    },\n    bind: function(f, scope, forceArgs){\n      return function() {return f.apply(scope, forceArgs ? self.removeEventListener(fallbackEvent, fixEvent, false);\n          else self['on' + fallbackEvent] = null;\n        });\n      }\n    };\n\n    var fixEvent = function(e) {\n      var origEvent = e     if ('wheelDelta'  in origEvent) { e.deltaY = -origEvent.wheelDelta;  }\n      if ('wheelDeltaY' in origEvent) { e.deltaY = -origEvent.wheelDeltaY; }\n      if ('wheelDeltaX' in origEvent) { e.deltaX = -origEvent.wheelDeltaX; }\n\n      // modern wheel event handler\n      if ('deltaY' in origEvent) {\n        e.deltaY = origEvent.deltaY;\n      }\n      if ('deltaX' in origEvent) {\n        e.deltaX = origEvent.deltaX;\n      }\n\n      // handle deltaMode for mouse wheel\n      e.delta = e.deltaY || e.deltaX;\n      if (origEvent.deltaMode === 1) {\n        var lineHeight = 16;\n        e.delta *= lineHeight;\n        e.deltaY *= lineHeight;\n        e.deltaX *= lineHeight;\n      }\n\n      return ($.event.dispatch || $.event.handle).call(this, e);\n    };\n  }());\n\n  // extra module methods\n  var moduleMixin = {\n    // provide function for firing native events\n    fireNativeEvent: function(elements, eventName) {\n      $(elements).each(function() {\n        var element = this, eventObject;\n        if (element.dispatchEvent) {\n          eventObject = document.createEvent('HTMLEvents');\n          eventObject.initEvent(eventName, true, true);\n          element.dispatchEvent(eventObject);\n        } else if (document.createEventObject) {\n          eventObject = document.createEventObject();\n          eventObject.target = element;\n          element.fireEvent('on' + eventName, eventObject);\n        }\n      });\n    },\n    // bind event handlers for module instance (functions beggining with \"on\")\n    bindHandlers: function() {\n      var self = this;\n      $.each(self, function(propName, propValue) {\n        if (propName.indexOf('on') === 0 && $.isFunction(propValue)) {\n          // dont use $.proxy here because it doesn't create unique handler\n          self[propName] = function() {\n            return propValue.apply(self, arguments);\n          };\n        }\n      });\n    }\n  };\n\n  // public API\n  var api = {\n    version: version,\n    modules: {},\n    getOptions: function() {\n      return $.extend({}, commonOptions);\n    },\n    setOptions: function(moduleName, moduleOptions) {\n      if (arguments.length > 1) {\n        // set module options\n        if (this.modules[moduleName]) {\n          $.extend(this.modules[moduleName].prototype.options, moduleOptions);\n        }\n      } else {\n        // set common options\n        $.extend(commonOptions, moduleName);\n      }\n    },\n    addModule: function(proto) {\n      // add module to list\n      var Module = function(options) {\n        // save instance to collection\n        if (!options.element.data(commonOptions.dataKey)) {\n          options.element.data(commonOptions.dataKey, this);\n        }\n        customInstances.push(this);\n\n        // save options\n        this.options = $.extend({}, commonOptions, this.options, getInlineOptions(options.element), options);\n\n        // bind event handlers to instance\n        this.bindHandlers();\n\n        // call constructor\n        this.init.apply(this, arguments);\n      };\n\n      // parse options from HTML attribute\n      var getInlineOptions = function(element) {\n        var dataOptions = element.data(commonOptions.optionsKey),\n          attrOptions = element.attr(commonOptions.optionsKey);\n\n        if (dataOptions) {\n          return dataOptions;\n        } else if (attrOptions) {\n          try {\n            return $.parseJSON(attrOptions);\n          } catch (e) {\n            // ignore invalid attributes\n          }\n        }\n      };\n\n      // set proto as prototype for new module\n      Module.prototype = proto;\n\n      // add mixin methods to module proto\n      $.extend(proto, moduleMixin);\n      if (proto.plugins) {\n        $.each(proto.plugins, function(pluginName, plugin) {\n          $.extend(plugin.prototype, moduleMixin);\n        });\n      }\n\n      // override destroy method\n      var originalDestroy = Module.prototype.destroy;\n      Module.prototype.destroy = function() {\n        this.options.element.removeData(this.options.dataKey);\n\n        for (var i = customInstances.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n          if (customInstances[i] === this) {\n            customInstances.splice(i, 1);\n            break;\n          }\n        }\n\n        if (originalDestroy) {\n          originalDestroy.apply(this, arguments);\n        }\n      };\n\n      // save module to list\n      this.modules[proto.name] = Module;\n    },\n    getInstance: function(element) {\n      return $(element).data(commonOptions.dataKey);\n    },\n    replace: function(elements, moduleName, customOptions) {\n      var self = this,\n        instance;\n\n      if (!commonOptions.styleSheetCreated) {\n        createStyleSheet();\n      }\n\n      $(elements).each(function() {\n        var moduleOptions,\n          element = $(this);\n\n        instance = element.data(commonOptions.dataKey);\n        if (instance) {\n          instance.refresh();\n        } else {\n          if (!moduleName) {\n            $.each(self.modules, function(currentModuleName, module) {\n              if (module.prototype.matchElement.call(module.prototype, element)) {\n                moduleName = currentModuleName;\n                return false;\n              }\n            });\n          }\n          if (moduleName) {\n            moduleOptions = $.extend({ element: element }, customOptions);\n            instance = new self.modules[moduleName](moduleOptions);\n          }\n        }\n      });\n      return instance;\n    },\n    refresh: function(elements) {\n      $(elements).each(function() {\n        var instance = $(this).data(commonOptions.dataKey);\n        if (instance) {\n          instance.refresh();\n        }\n      });\n    },\n    destroy: function(elements) {\n      $(elements).each(function() {\n        var instance = $(this).data(commonOptions.dataKey);\n        if (instance) {\n          instance.destroy();\n        }\n      });\n    },\n    replaceAll: (this.className.indexOf('jcf-ignore') < 0) {\n            self.replace(this, moduleName);\n          }\n        });\n      });\n    },\n    refreshAll: function(context) {\n      if (context) {\n if (instance) {\n              instance.refresh();\n            }\n          });\n        });\n      } else {\n        for (var i = customInstances.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n          customInstances[i].refresh();\n        }\n      }\n    },\n    destroyAll: function(context) {\n      if (context) {\n        $.each(this.modules, function(moduleName, module) {\n          $(module.prototype.selector, context).each(function(index, element) {\n            var instance = $(element).data(commonOptions.dataKey);\n            if (instance) {\n              instance.destroy();\n            }\n          });\n        });\n      } else {\n        while (customInstances.length) {\n          customInstances[0].destroy();\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  };\n\n  // always export API to the global window object\n  window.jcf = api;\n\n  return api;\n}));\n\n/*!\n * JavaScript Custom Forms : Select Module\n *\n * Copyright 2014-2015 PSD2HTML - 'jcf-scroll-active'\n    }, options);\n    this.init();\n  }\n  $.extend(SelectList.prototype, {\n    init: function() {\n      this.initStructure();\n      this.refreshSelectedClass();\n this.element.prop('selectedIndex');\n      this.rebuildList();\n    },\n    attachEvents: function() {\n      this.bindHandlers();\n      this.listHolder.on('jcf-pointerdown', this.indexSelector, this.onItemPress);\n      this.listHolder.on('jcf-pointerdown', this.onPress);\n\n      if (this.options.useHoverClass) {\n        this.listHolder.on('jcf-pointerover', this.indexSelector, this.onHoverItem);\n      }\n    },\n    onPress: function(e) {\n      $(this).trigger('press', e);\n      this.listHolder.on('jcf-pointerup', this.onRelease);\n    },\n    onRelease: function(e) {\n      $(this).trigger('release', e);\n      this.listHolder.off('jcf-pointerup', this.onRelease);\n    },\n    onHoverItem: function(e) {\n      var hoverIndex = parseFloat(e.currentTarget.getAttribute(this.options.indexAttribute));\n      this.fakeOptions.removeClass(this.options.hoverClass).eq(hoverIndex).addClass(this.options.hoverClass);\n    },\n    onItemPress: function(e) {\n      if (e.pointerType === 'touch' || this.options.selectOnClick) {\n        // select option after \"click\"\n        this.tmpListOffsetTop = this.list.offset().top;\n        this.listHolder.on('jcf-pointerup', this.indexSelector, this.onItemRelease);\n      } else {\n        // select option immediately\n        this.onSelectItem(e);\n      }\n    },\n    onItemRelease: function(e) {\n      // remove event handlers and temporary data\n      this.listHolder.off('jcf-pointerup', this.indexSelector, this.onItemRelease);\n\n      // simulate item selection\n      if (this.tmpListOffsetTop === this.list.offset().top) {\n        this.listHolder.on('click', this.indexSelector, { savedPointerType: e.pointerType }, this.onSelectItem);\n      }\n      delete this.tmpListOffsetTop;\n    },\n    onSelectItem: function(e) {\n      var clickedIndex = parseFloat(e.currentTarget.getAttribute(this.options.indexAttribute)),\n        pointerType = e.data && e.data.savedPointerType || e.pointerType || 'mouse',\n        range;\n\n      // remove click event handler\n      this.listHolder.off('click', this.indexSelector, this.onSelectItem);\n\n      // ignore clicks on disabled options\n      if (e.button > 1 || this.realOptions[clickedIndex].disabled) {\n        return;\n      }\n\n      if (this.element.prop('multiple')) {\n        if (e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey || pointerType === 'touch' || this.options.multipleSelectWithoutKey) {\n          // if CTRL/CMD pressed or touch devices - toggle selected option\n          this.realOptions[clickedIndex].selected = !this.realOptions[clickedIndex].selected;\n        } else if (e.shiftKey) {\n          // if SHIFT pressed - update selection\n          range = [this.lastClickedIndex, clickedIndex].sort(function(a, b) {\n            return a - b;\n          });\n          this.realOptions.each(function(index, option) {\n            option.selected = (index >= range[0] && index <= range[1]);\n          });\n        } else {\n          // set single selected index\n          this.element.prop('selectedIndex', clickedIndex);\n        }\n      } else {\n        this.element.prop('selectedIndex', clickedIndex);\n      }\n\n      // save last clicked option\n      if (!e.shiftKey) {\n        this.lastClickedIndex = clickedIndex;\n      }\n\n      // refresh classes\n      this.refreshSelectedClass();\n\n      // scroll to active item in desktop browsers\n      if (pointerType === 'mouse') {\n        this.scrollToActiveOption();\n      }\n\n      // make callback when item selected\n      $(this).trigger('select');\n    },\n    rebuildList: function() {\n      // rebuild options\n      var self = this,\n        rootElement = this.element[0];\n\n      // recursively create fake options\n      this.storedSelectHTML = rootElement.innerHTML;\n      this.optionIndex = 0;\n      this.list = $(this.createOptionsList(rootElement));\n      this.listHolder.empty().append(this.list);\n      this.realOptions = this.element.find('option');\n      this.fakeOptions = this.list.find(this.indexSelector);\n      this.fakeListItems = this.list.find('.' + this.options.captionClass + ',' + this.indexSelector);\n      delete this.optionIndex;\n\n      // detect max visible items\n      var maxCount = this.options.maxVisibleItems,\n        sizeValue = this.element.prop('size');\n      if (sizeValue > 1 && !this.element.is('[jcf-size]')) {\n        maxCount = sizeValue;\n      }\n\n      // handle scrollbar\n      var needScrollBar = this.fakeOptions.length > maxCount;\n      this.container.toggleClass(this.options.scrollClass, needScrollBar);\n      if (needScrollBar) {\n        // change max-height\n        this.listHolder.css({\n          maxHeight: this.getOverflowHeight(maxCount),\n          overflow: 'auto'\n        });\n\n        if (this.options.useCustomScroll && jcf.modules.Scrollable) {\n          // add custom scrollbar if specified in options\n          jcf.replace(this.listHolder, 'Scrollable', {\n            handleResize: this.options.handleResize,\n            alwaysPreventMouseWheel: this.options.alwaysPreventMouseWheel\n          });\n          return;\n        }\n      }\n\n      // disable edge wheel scrolling\n      if (this.options.alwaysPreventMouseWheel) {\n        this.preventWheelHandler = function(e) {\n          var currentScrollTop = self.listHolder.scrollTop(),\n            maxScrollTop = self.listHolder.prop('scrollHeight') - self.listHolder.innerHeight();\n\n          // check edge cases\n          if ((currentScrollTop <= 0 && e.deltaY < 0) || (currentScrollTop >= maxScrollTop && e.deltaY > 0)) {\n            e.preventDefault();\n          }\n        };\n        this.listHolder.on('jcf-mousewheel', this.preventWheelHandler);\n      }\n    },\n    refreshSelectedClass: function() {\n      var self = this,\n        selectedItem,\n        isMultiple = this.element.prop('multiple'),\n        selectedIndex = this.element.prop('selectedIndex');\n\n      if (isMultiple) {\n        this.realOptions.each(function(index, option) {\n          self.fakeOptions.eq(index).toggleClass(self.options.selectedClass, !!option.selected);\n        });\n      } else {\n        this.fakeOptions.removeClass(this.options.selectedClass + ' ' + this.options.hoverClass);\n        selectedItem = this.fakeOptions.eq(selectedIndex).addClass(this.options.selectedClass);\n        if (this.options.useHoverClass) {\n          selectedItem.addClass(this.options.hoverClass);\n        }\n      }\n    },\n    scrollToActiveOption: function() {\n      // scroll to target option\n      var targetOffset = this.getActiveOptionOffset();\n      if (typeof targetOffset === 'number') {\n        this.listHolder.prop('scrollTop', targetOffset);\n      }\n    },\n    getSelectedIndexRange: function() {\n      var firstSelected = -1, lastSelected = -1;\n      this.realOptions.each(function(index, option) {\n        if (option.selected) {\n          if (firstSelected < 0) {\n            firstSelected = index;\n          }\n          lastSelected = index;\n        }\n      });\n      return [firstSelected, lastSelected];\n    },\n    getChangedSelectedIndex: function() {\n      var selectedIndex = this.element.prop('selectedIndex'),\n        targetIndex;\n\n      if (this.element.prop('multiple')) {\n        // multiple selects handling\n        if (!this.previousRange) {\n          this.previousRange = [selectedIndex, selectedIndex];\n        }\n        this.currentRange = this.getSelectedIndexRange();\n        targetIndex = this.currentRange[this.currentRange[0] !== this.previousRange[0] ? 0 : 1];\n        this.previousRange = this.currentRange;\n        return targetIndex;\n      } else {\n        // single choice selects handling\n        return selectedIndex;\n      }\n    },\n    getActiveOptionOffset: function() {\n      // calc values\n      var dropHeight = this.listHolder.height(),\n        dropScrollTop = this.listHolder.prop('scrollTop'),\n        currentIndex = this.getChangedSelectedIndex(),\n        fakeOption = this.fakeOptions.eq(currentIndex),\n        fakeOptionOffset = fakeOption.offset().top - this.list.offset().top,\n        fakeOptionHeight = fakeOption.innerHeight();\n\n      // scroll list\n      if (fakeOptionOffset + fakeOptionHeight >= dropScrollTop + dropHeight) {\n        // scroll down (always scroll to option)\n        return fakeOptionOffset - dropHeight + fakeOptionHeight;\n      } else if (fakeOptionOffset < dropScrollTop) {\n        // scroll up to option\n        return fakeOptionOffset;\n      }\n    },\n    getOverflowHeight: function(sizeValue) {\n      var item = this.fakeListItems.eq(sizeValue - 1),\n        listOffset = this.list.offset().top,\n        itemOffset = item.offset().top,\n        itemHeight = item.innerHeight();\n\n      return itemOffset + itemHeight - listOffset;\n    },\n    getScrollTop: function() {\n      return this.listHolder.scrollTop();\n    },\n    setScrollTop: function(value) {\n      this.listHolder.scrollTop(value);\n    },\n    createOption: function(option) {\n      var newOption = document.createElement('span');\n      newOption.className = this.options.optionClass;\n      newOption.innerHTML = option.innerHTML;\n      newOption.setAttribute(this.options.indexAttribute, this.optionIndex++);\n\n      var optionImage, optionImageSrc = option.getAttribute('data-image');\n      if (optionImageSrc) {\n        optionImage = document.createElement('img');\n        optionImage.src = optionImageSrc;\n        newOption.insertBefore(optionImage, newOption.childNodes[0]);\n      }\n      if (option.disabled) {\n        newOption.className += ' ' + this.options.disabledClass;\n      }\n      if (option.className) {\n        newOption.className += ' ' + getPrefixedClasses(option.className, this.options.cloneClassPrefix);\n      }\n      return newOption;\n    },\n    createOptGroup: function(optgroup) {\n      var optGroupContainer = document.createElement('span'),\n        optGroupName = optgroup.getAttribute('label'),\n        optGroupCaption, optGroupList;\n\n      // create caption\n      optGroupCaption = document.createElement('span');\n      optGroupCaption.className = this.options.captionClass;\n      optGroupCaption.innerHTML = optGroupName;\n      optGroupContainer.appendChild(optGroupCaption);\n\n      // create list of options\n      if (optgroup.children.length) {\n        optGroupList = this.createOptionsList(optgroup);\n        optGroupContainer.appendChild(optGroupList);\n      }\n\n      optGroupContainer.className = this.options.groupClass;\n      return optGroupContainer;\n newNode;\n\n        switch (currentNode.tagName.toLowerCase()) {\n          case 'option': newNode = self.createOption(currentNode); break;\n          case 'optgroup': newNode = self.createOptGroup(currentNode); break;\n        }\n        list.appendChild(item).appendChild(newNode);\n      });\n      return list;\n    },\n    refresh: function() {\n      // check for select innerHTML changes\n      if (this.storedSelectHTML !== this.element.prop('innerHTML')) {\n        this.rebuildList();\n      }\n\n      // refresh custom scrollbar\n      var scrollInstance = jcf.getInstance(this.listHolder);\n      if (scrollInstance) {\n        scrollInstance.refresh();\n      }\n\n      // refresh selectes classes\n      this.refreshSelectedClass();\n    },\n    destroy: function() {\n      this.listHolder.off('jcf-mousewheel', this.preventWheelHandler);\n      this.listHolder.off('jcf-pointerdown', this.indexSelector, this.onSelectItem);\n      this.listHolder.off('jcf-pointerover', this.indexSelector, this.onHoverItem);\n      this.listHolder.off('jcf-pointerdown', this.onPress);\n    }\n  });\n\n  // helper functions\n  var   var unselectableClass = jcf.getOptions().unselectableClass;\n    function preventHandler(e) {\n      e.preventDefault();\n    }\n    return function(node) {\n      node.addClass(unselectableClass).on('selectstart', preventHandler);\n    };\n  }());\n\n}(jQuery, this));\n\n/*!\n * JavaScript Custom Forms : Scrollbar Module\n *\n * Copyright 2014-2015 PSD2HTML - http://psd2html.com/jcf\n * Released under the MIT license (LICENSE.txt)\n *\n * Version: 1.1.3\n */\n;(function($, window) {\n  'use strict';\n\n  jcf.addModule({\n    name: 'Scrollable',\n    selector: '.jcf-scrollable',\n    plugins: {\n      ScrollBar: ScrollBar\n    },\n    options: {\n      mouseWheelStep: 150,\n      handleResize: true,\n      alwaysShowScrollbars: false,\n      alwaysPreventMouseWheel: false,\n      scrollAreaStructure: '<div class=\"jcf-scrollable-wrapper\"></div>'\n    },\n    matchElement: function(element) {\n      return element.is('.jcf-scrollable');\n    },\n    init: function() {\n      this.initStructure();\n      this.attachEvents();\n      this.rebuildScrollbars();\n    },\n    initStructure: function() {\n      // prepare structure\n      this.doc = $(document);\n      this.win = $(window);\n      this.realElement = $(this.options.element);\n      this.scrollWrapper = $(this.options.scrollAreaStructure).insertAfter(this.realElement);\n\n      // set initial styles\n      this.scrollWrapper.css('position', 'relative');\n      this.realElement.css('overflow', 'hidden');\n      this.vBarEdge = 0;\n    },\n    attachEvents: function() {\n      // create scrollbars\n      var self = this;\n      this.vBar = new ScrollBar({\n        holder: this.scrollWrapper,\n        vertical: true,\n        onScroll: function(scrollTop) {\n          self.realElement.scrollTop(scrollTop);\n        }\n      });\n      this.hBar = new ScrollBar({\n        holder: this.scrollWrapper,\n        vertical: false,\n        onScroll: function(scrollLeft) {\n          self.realElement.scrollLeft(scrollLeft);\n        }\n      });\n\n      // add event handlers\n      this.realElement.on('scroll', this.onScroll);\n      if (this.options.handleResize) {\n        this.win.on('resize orientationchange load', this.onResize);\n      }\n\n      // add pointer/wheel event handlers\n      this.realElement.on('jcf-mousewheel', this.onMouseWheel);\n      this.realElement.on('jcf-pointerdown', this.onTouchBody);\n    },\n    onScroll: function() {\n      this.redrawScrollbars();\n    },\n    onResize: function() {\n      // do not rebuild scrollbars if form field is in focus\n      if (!$(document.activeElement).is(':input')) {\n        this.rebuildScrollbars();\n      }\n    },\n    onTouchBody: function(e) {\n      if (e.pointerType === 'touch') {\n        this.touchData = {\n          scrollTop: this.realElement.scrollTop(),\n          scrollLeft: this.realElement.scrollLeft(),\n          left: e.pageX,\n          top: e.pageY\n        };\n        this.doc.on({\n          'jcf-pointermove': this.onMoveBody,\n          'jcf-pointerup': this.onReleaseBody\n        });\n      }\n    },\n    onMoveBody: function(e) {\n      var targetScrollTop,\n        targetScrollLeft,\n        verticalScrollAllowed = this.verticalScrollActive,\n        horizontalScrollAllowed = this.horizontalScrollActive;\n\n      if (e.pointerType === 'touch') {\n        targetScrollTop = this.touchData.scrollTop - e.pageY + this.touchData.top;\n        targetScrollLeft = this.touchData.scrollLeft - e.pageX + this.touchData.left;\n\n        // check that scrolling is ended and release outer scrolling\n        if (this.verticalScrollActive && (targetScrollTop < 0 || targetScrollTop > this.vBar.maxValue)) {\n          verticalScrollAllowed = false;\n        }\n        if (this.horizontalScrollActive && (targetScrollLeft < 0 || targetScrollLeft > this.hBar.maxValue)) {\n          horizontalScrollAllowed = false;\n        }\n\n        this.realElement.scrollTop(targetScrollTop);\n        this.realElement.scrollLeft(targetScrollLeft);\n\n        if (verticalScrollAllowed || horizontalScrollAllowed) {\n          e.preventDefault();\n        } else {\n          this.onReleaseBody(e);\n        }\n      }\n    },\n    onReleaseBody: function(e) {\n      if (e.pointerType === 'touch') {\n        delete this.touchData;\n        this.doc.off({\n          'jcf-pointermove': this.onMoveBody,\n          'jcf-pointerup': this.onReleaseBody\n        });\n      }\n    },\n    onMouseWheel: function(e) {\n      var currentScrollTop = this.realElement.scrollTop(),\n        currentScrollLeft = this.realElement.scrollLeft(),\n        maxScrollTop = this.realElement.prop('scrollHeight') - this.embeddedDimensions.innerHeight,\n        maxScrollLeft = this.realElement.prop('scrollWidth') - this.embeddedDimensions.innerWidth,\n        extraLeft, extraTop, preventFlag;\n\n      // check edge cases\n      if (!this.options.alwaysPreventMouseWheel) {\n        if (this.verticalScrollActive && e.deltaY) {\n          if (!(currentScrollTop <= 0 && e.deltaY < 0) && !(currentScrollTop >= maxScrollTop && e.deltaY > 0)) {\n            preventFlag = true;\n          }\n        }\n        if (this.horizontalScrollActive && e.deltaX) {\n          if (!(currentScrollLeft <= 0 && e.deltaX < 0) && !(currentScrollLeft >= maxScrollLeft && e.deltaX > 0)) {\n            preventFlag = true;\n          }\n        }\n        if (!this.verticalScrollActive && !this.horizontalScrollActive) {\n          return;\n        }\n      }\n\n      // prevent default action and scroll item\n      if (preventFlag || this.options.alwaysPreventMouseWheel) {\n        e.preventDefault();\n      } else {\n        return;\n      }\n\n      extraLeft = e.deltaX / 100 * this.options.mouseWheelStep;\n      extraTop = e.deltaY / 100 * this.options.mouseWheelStep;\n\n      this.realElement.scrollTop(currentScrollTop + extraTop);\n      this.realElement.scrollLeft(currentScrollLeft + extraLeft);\n    },\n    setScrollBarEdge: function(edgeSize) {\n      this.vBarEdge = edgeSize || 0;\n      this.redrawScrollbars();\n    },\n    saveElementDimensions: function() {\n      this.savedDimensions = {\n        top: this.realElement.width(),\n        left: this.realElement.height()\n      };\n      return this;\n    },\n    restoreElementDimensions: function() {\n      if (this.savedDimensions) {\n        this.realElement.css({\n          width: this.savedDimensions.width,\n          height: this.savedDimensions.height\n        });\n      }\n      return this;\n    },\n    saveScrollOffsets: function() {\n      this.savedOffsets = {\n        top: this.realElement.scrollTop(),\n        left: this.realElement.scrollLeft()\n      };\n      return this;\n    },\n    restoreScrollOffsets: function() {\n      if (this.savedOffsets) {\n        this.realElement.scrollTop(this.savedOffsets.top);\n        this.realElement.scrollLeft(this.savedOffsets.left);\n      }\n      return this;\n    },\n    getContainerDimensions: function() {\n      // save current styles\n      var desiredDimensions,\n        currentStyles,\n        currentHeight,\n        currentWidth;\n\n      if (this.isModifiedStyles) {\n        desiredDimensions = {\n          width: this.realElement.innerWidth() + this.vBar.getThickness(),\n          height: this.realElement.innerHeight() + this.hBar.getThickness()\n        };\n      } else {\n        // unwrap real element and measure it according to CSS\n        this.saveElementDimensions().saveScrollOffsets();\n        this.realElement.insertAfter(this.scrollWrapper);\n        this.scrollWrapper.detach();\n\n        // measure element\n        currentStyles = this.realElement.prop('style');\n        currentWidth = parseFloat(currentStyles.width);\n        currentHeight = parseFloat(currentStyles.height);\n\n        // reset styles if needed\n        if (this.embeddedDimensions && currentWidth && currentHeight) {\n          this.isModifiedStyles |= (currentWidth !== this.embeddedDimensions.width || currentHeight !== this.embeddedDimensions.height);\n          this.realElement.css({\n            overflow: '',\n            width: '',\n            height: ''\n          });\n        }\n\n        // calculate desired dimensions for real element\n        desiredDimensions = {\n          width: this.realElement.outerWidth(),\n          height: this.realElement.outerHeight()\n        };\n\n        // restore structure and original scroll offsets\n        this.scrollWrapper.insertAfter(this.realElement);\n        this.realElement.css('overflow', 'hidden').prependTo(this.scrollWrapper);\n        this.restoreElementDimensions().restoreScrollOffsets();\n      }\n\n      return desiredDimensions;\n    },\n    getEmbeddedDimensions: function(dimensions) {\n      // handle \\rs cropping\n      var fakeBarWidth = this.vBar.getThickness(),\n        fakeBarHeight = this.hBar.getThickness(),\n        paddingWidth = this.realElement.outerWidth() - this.realElement.width(),\n        paddingHeight = this.realElement.outerHeight() - this.realElement.height(),\n        resultDimensions;\n\n      if (this.options.alwaysShowScrollbars) {\n        // simply return dimensions without custom scrollbars\n        this.verticalScrollActive = true;\n        this.horizontalScrollActive = true;\n        resultDimensions = {\n          innerWidth: dimensions.width - fakeBarWidth,\n          innerHeight: dimensions.height - fakeBarHeight\n        };\n      } else {\n        // detect when to display each scrollbar\n        this.saveElementDimensions();\n        this.verticalScrollActive = false;\n        this.horizontalScrollActive = false;\n\n        // fill container with full size\n        this.realElement.css({\n          width: dimensions.width - paddingWidth,\n          height: dimensions.height - paddingHeight\n        });\n\n        this.horizontalScrollActive = this.realElement.prop('scrollWidth') > this.containerDimensions.width;\n        this.verticalScrollActive = this.realElement.prop('scrollHeight') > this.containerDimensions.height;\n\n        this.restoreElementDimensions();\n        resultDimensions = {\n          innerWidth: dimensions.width - (this.verticalScrollActive ? fakeBarWidth : 0),\n          innerHeight: dimensions.height - (this.horizontalScrollActive ? fakeBarHeight : 0)\n        };\n      }\n      $.extend(resultDimensions, {\n        width: resultDimensions.innerWidth - paddingWidth,\n        height: resultDimensions.innerHeight - paddingHeight\n      });\n      return resultDimensions;\n    },\n    rebuildScrollbars: function() {\n      // resize wrapper according to real element styles\n      this.containerDimensions = this.getContainerDimensions();\n      this.embeddedDimensions = this.getEmbeddedDimensions(this.containerDimensions);\n\n      // resize wrapper to desired dimensions\n      this.scrollWrapper.css({\n        width: this.containerDimensions.width,\n        height: this.containerDimensions.height\n      });\n\n      // resize element inside wrapper excluding scrollbar size\n      this.realElement.css({\n        overflow: 'hidden',\n        width: this.embeddedDimensions.width,\n        height: this.embeddedDimensions.height\n      });\n\n      // redraw scrollbar offset\n      this.redrawScrollbars();\n    },\n    redrawScrollbars: function() {\n      var viewSize, maxScrollValue;\n\n      // redraw vertical scrollbar\n      if (this.verticalScrollActive) {\n        viewSize = this.vBarEdge ? this.containerDimensions.height - this.vBarEdge : this.embeddedDimensions.innerHeight;\n        maxScrollValue = Math.max(this.realElement.prop('offsetHeight'), this.realElement.prop('scrollHeight')) - this.vBarEdge;\n\n        this.vBar.show().setMaxValue(maxScrollValue - viewSize).setRatio(viewSize / maxScrollValue).setSize(viewSize);\n        this.vBar.setValue(this.realElement.scrollTop());\n      } else {\n        this.vBar.hide();\n      }\n\n      // redraw horizontal scrollbar\n      if (this.horizontalScrollActive) {\n        viewSize = this.embeddedDimensions.innerWidth;\n        maxScrollValue = this.realElement.prop('scrollWidth');\n\n        if (maxScrollValue === viewSize) {\n          this.horizontalScrollActive = false;\n        }\n        this.hBar.show().setMaxValue(maxScrollValue - viewSize).setRatio(viewSize / maxScrollValue).setSize(viewSize);\n        this.hBar.setValue(this.realElement.scrollLeft());\n      } else {\n        this.hBar.hide();\n      }\n\n      // set \"touch-action\" style rule\n      var touchAction = '';\n      if (this.verticalScrollActive && this.horizontalScrollActive) {\n        touchAction = 'none';\n      } else if (this.verticalScrollActive) {\n        touchAction = 'pan-x';\n      } else if (this.horizontalScrollActive) {\n        touchAction = 'pan-y';\n      }\n      this.realElement.css('touchAction', touchAction);\n    },\n    refresh: function() {\n      this.rebuildScrollbars();\n    },\n    destroy: function() {\n      // remove event listeners\n      this.win.off('resize orientationchange load', this.onResize);\n      this.realElement.off({\n        'jcf-mousewheel': this.onMouseWheel,\n        'jcf-pointerdown': this.onTouchBody\n      });\n      this.doc.off({\n        'jcf-pointermove': this.onMoveBody,\n        'jcf-pointerup': this.onReleaseBody\n      });\n\n      // restore structure\n      this.saveScrollOffsets();\n      this.vBar.destroy();\n      this.hBar.destroy();\n      this.realElement.insertAfter(this.scrollWrapper).css({\n        touchAction: '',\n        overflow: '',\n        width: '',\n        height: ''\n      });\n      this.scrollWrapper.remove();\n      this.restoreScrollOffsets();\n    }\n  });\n\n  // custom scrollbar\n  function ScrollBar(options) {\n    this.options = $.extend({\n      holder: null,\n      vertical: true,\n      inactiveClass: 'jcf-inactive',\n      verticalClass: 'jcf-scrollbar-vertical',\n      horizontalClass: 'jcf-scrollbar-horizontal',\n      scrollbarStructure: '<div class=\"jcf-scrollbar\"><div class=\"jcf-scrollbar-dec\"></div><div class=\"jcf-scrollbar-slider\"><div class=\"jcf-scrollbar-handle\"></div></div><div class=\"jcf-scrollbar-inc\"></div></div>',\n      btnDecSelector: '.jcf-scrollbar-dec',\n      btnIncSelector: '.jcf-scrollbar-inc',\n      sliderSelector: '.jcf-scrollbar-slider',\n      handleSelector: '.jcf-scrollbar-handle',\n      scrollInterval: 300,\n      scrollStep: 400 // px/sec\n    }, options);\n    this.init();\n  }\n  $.extend(ScrollBar.prototype, {\n    init: function() {\n      this.initStructure();\n      this.attachEvents();\n    },\n    initStructure: function() {\n      // define proporties\n      this.doc = $(document);\n      this.isVertical = !!this.options.vertical;\n      this.sizeProperty = this.isVertical ? 'height' : 'width';\n      this.fullSizeProperty = this.isVertical ? 'outerHeight' : 'outerWidth';\n      this.invertedSizeProperty = this.isVertical ? 'width' : 'height';\n      this.thicknessMeasureMethod = 'outer' + this.invertedSizeProperty.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + this.invertedSizeProperty.substr(1);\n      this.offsetProperty = this.isVertical ?
